</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">foo</code>和<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">bar</code>都是 Generator 函数，在<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">bar</code>里面调用<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">foo</code>，是不会有效果的。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">这个就需要用到<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">yield*</code>语句，用来在一个 Generator 函数里面执行另一个 Generator 函数。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">function* bar() {
  yield 'x';
  yield* foo();
  yield 'y';
}

// 等同于
function* bar() {
  yield 'x';
  yield 'a';
  yield 'b';
  yield 'y';
}

// 等同于
function* bar() {
  yield 'x';
  for (let v of foo()) {
    yield v;
  }
  yield 'y';
}

for (let v of bar()){
  console.log(v);
}
// "x"
// "a"
// "b"
// "y"
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">再来看一个对比的例子。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">function* inner() {
  yield 'hello!';
}

function* outer1() {
  yield 'open';
  yield inner();
  yield 'close';
}

var gen = outer1()
gen.next().value // "open"
gen.next().value // 返回一个遍历器对象
gen.next().value // "close"

function* outer2() {
  yield 'open'
  yield* inner()
  yield 'close'
}

var gen = outer2()
gen.next().value // "open"
gen.next().value // "hello!"
gen.next().value // "close"
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面例子中，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">outer2</code>使用了<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">yield*</code>，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">outer1</code>没使用。结果就是，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">outer1</code>返回一个遍历器对象，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">outer2</code>返回该遍历器对象的内部值。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">从语法角度看，如果<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">yield</code>命令后面跟的是一个遍历器对象，需要在<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">yield</code>命令后面加上星号，表明它返回的是一个遍历器对象。这被称为<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">yield*</code>语句。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">let delegatedIterator = (function* () {
  yield 'Hello!';
  yield 'Bye!';
}());

let delegatingIterator = (function* () {
  yield 'Greetings!';
  yield* delegatedIterator;
  yield 'Ok, bye.';
}());

for(let value of delegatingIterator) {
  console.log(value);
}
// "Greetings!
// "Hello!"
// "Bye!"
// "Ok, bye."
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">delegatingIterator</code>是代理者，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">delegatedIterator</code>是被代理者。由于<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">yield* delegatedIterator</code>语句得到的值，是一个遍历器，所以要用星号表示。运行结果就是使用一个遍历器，遍历了多个Generator函数，有递归的效果。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;"><code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">yield*</code>后面的Generator函数（没有<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">return</code>语句时），等同于在Generator函数内部，部署一个<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">for...of</code>循环。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">function* concat(iter1, iter2) {
  yield* iter1;
  yield* iter2;
}

// 等同于

function* concat(iter1, iter2) {
  for (var value of iter1) {
    yield value;
  }
  for (var value of iter2) {
    yield value;
  }
}
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码说明，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">yield*</code>后面的Generator函数（没有<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">return</code>语句时），不过是<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">for...of</code>的一种简写形式，完全可以用后者替代前者。反之，则需要用<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">var value = yield* iterator</code>的形式获取<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">return</code>语句的值。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">如果<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">yield*</code>后面跟着一个数组，由于数组原生支持遍历器，因此就会遍历数组成员。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">function* gen(){
  yield* ["a", "b", "c"];
}

gen().next() // { value:"a", done:false }
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">yield</code>命令后面如果不加星号，返回的是整个数组，加了星号就表示返回的是数组的遍历器对象。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">实际上，任何数据结构只要有Iterator接口，就可以被<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">yield*</code>遍历。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">let read = (function* () {
  yield 'hello';
  yield* 'hello';
})();

read.next().value // "hello"
read.next().value // "h"
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">yield</code>语句返回整个字符串，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">yield*</code>语句返回单个字符。因为字符串具有Iterator接口，所以被<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">yield*</code>遍历。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">如果被代理的Generator函数有<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">return</code>语句，那么就可以向代理它的Generator函数返回数据。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">function *foo() {
  yield 2;
  yield 3;
  return "foo";
}

function *bar() {
  yield 1;
  var v = yield *foo();
  console.log( "v: " + v );
  yield 4;
}

var it = bar();

it.next()
// {value: 1, done: false}
it.next()
// {value: 2, done: false}
it.next()
// {value: 3, done: false}
it.next();
// "v: foo"
// {value: 4, done: false}
it.next()
// {value: undefined, done: true}
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码在第四次调用<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">next</code>方法的时候，屏幕上会有输出，这是因为函数<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">foo</code>的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">return</code>语句，向函数<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">bar</code>提供了返回值。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">再看一个例子。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">function* genFuncWithReturn() {
  yield 'a';
  yield 'b';
  return 'The result';
}
function* logReturned(genObj) {
  let result = yield* genObj;
  console.log(result);
}

[...logReturned(genFuncWithReturn())]
// The result
// 值为 [ 'a', 'b' ]
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，存在两次遍历。第一次是扩展运算符遍历函数<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">logReturned</code>返回的遍历器对象，第二次是<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">yield*</code>语句遍历函数<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">genFuncWithReturn</code>返回的遍历器对象。这两次遍历的效果是叠加的，最终表现为扩展运算符遍历函数<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">genFuncWithReturn</code>返回的遍历器对象。所以，最后的数据表达式得到的值等于<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">[ 'a', 'b' ]</code>。但是，函数<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">genFuncWithReturn</code>的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">return</code>语句的返回值<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">The result</code>，会返回给函数<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">logReturned</code>内部的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">result</code>变量，因此会有终端输出。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;"><code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">yield*</code>命令可以很方便地取出嵌套数组的所有成员。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">function* iterTree(tree) {
  if (Array.isArray(tree)) {
    for(let i=0; i &lt; tree.length; i++) {
      yield* iterTree(tree[i]);
    }
  } else {
    yield tree;
  }
}

const tree = [ 'a', ['b', 'c'], ['d', 'e'] ];

for(let x of iterTree(tree)) {
  console.log(x);
}
// a
// b
// c
// d
// e
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">下面是一个稍微复杂的例子，使用<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">yield*</code>语句遍历完全二叉树。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">// 下面是二叉树的构造函数，
// 三个参数分别是左树、当前节点和右树
function Tree(left, label, right) {
  this.left = left;
  this.label = label;
  this.right = right;
}

// 下面是中序（inorder）遍历函数。
// 由于返回的是一个遍历器，所以要用generator函数。
// 函数体内采用递归算法，所以左树和右树要用yield*遍历
function* inorder(t) {
  if (t) {
    yield* inorder(t.left);
    yield t.label;
    yield* inorder(t.right);
  }
}

// 下面生成二叉树
function make(array) {
  // 判断是否为叶节点
  if (array.length == 1) return new Tree(null, array[0], null);
  return new Tree(make(array[0]), array[1], make(array[2]));
}
let tree = make([[['a'], 'b', ['c']], 'd', [['e'], 'f', ['g']]]);

// 遍历二叉树
var result = [];
for (let node of inorder(tree)) {
  result.push(node);
}

result
// ['a', 'b', 'c', 'd', 'e', 'f', 'g']
</code></pre><h2 id="-generator-" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 24px 0px 16px; padding: 0px 0px 0.3em; top: -900em; left: -900em; box-sizing: border-box; border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(238, 238, 238); line-height: 1.25; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">作为对象属性的Generator函数</h2><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">如果一个对象的属性是Generator函数，可以简写成下面的形式。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">let obj = {
  * myGeneratorMethod() {
    ···
  }
};
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">myGeneratorMethod</code>属性前面有一个星号，表示这个属性是一个Generator函数。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">它的完整形式如下，与上面的写法是等价的。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">let obj = {
  myGeneratorMethod: function* () {
    // ···
  }
};
</code></pre><h2 id="generator-this-" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 24px 0px 16px; padding: 0px 0px 0.3em; top: -900em; left: -900em; box-sizing: border-box; border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(238, 238, 238); line-height: 1.25; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">Generator函数的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; font-weight: 400; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 17.85px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">this</code></h2><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">Generator函数总是返回一个遍历器，ES6规定这个遍历器是Generator函数的实例，也继承了Generator函数的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">prototype</code>对象上的方法。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">function* g() {}

g.prototype.hello = function () {
  return 'hi!';
};

let obj = g();

obj instanceof g // true
obj.hello() // 'hi!'
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码表明，Generator函数<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">g</code>返回的遍历器<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">obj</code>，是<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">g</code>的实例，而且继承了<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">g.prototype</code>。但是，如果把<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">g</code>当作普通的构造函数，并不会生效，因为<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">g</code>返回的总是遍历器对象，而不是<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">this</code>对象。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">function* g() {
  this.a = 11;
}

let obj = g();
obj.a // undefined
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，Generator函数<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">g</code>在<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">this</code>对象上面添加了一个属性<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">a</code>，但是<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">obj</code>对象拿不到这个属性。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">Generator函数也不能跟<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">new</code>命令一起用，会报错。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">function* F() {
  yield this.x = 2;
  yield this.y = 3;
}

new F()
// TypeError: F is not a constructor
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">new</code>命令跟构造函数<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">F</code>一起使用，结果报错，因为<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">F</code>不是构造函数。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">那么，有没有办法让Generator函数返回一个正常的对象实例，既可以用<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">next</code>方法，又可以获得正常的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">this</code>？</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">下面是一个变通方法。首先，生成一个空对象，使用<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">call</code>方法绑定Generator函数内部的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">this</code>。这样，构造函数调用以后，这个空对象就是Generator函数的实例对象了。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">function* F() {
  this.a = 1;
  yield this.b = 2;
  yield this.c = 3;
}
var obj = {};
var f = F.call(obj);

f.next();  // Object {value: 2, done: false}
f.next();  // Object {value: 3, done: false}
f.next();  // Object {value: undefined, done: true}

obj.a // 1
obj.b // 2
obj.c // 3
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，首先是<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">F</code>内部的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">this</code>对象绑定<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">obj</code>对象，然后调用它，返回一个Iterator对象。这个对象执行三次<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">next</code>方法（因为<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">F</code>内部有两个<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">yield</code>语句），完成F内部所有代码的运行。这时，所有内部属性都绑定在<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">obj</code>对象上了，因此<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">obj</code>对象也就成了<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">F</code>的实例。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，执行的是遍历器对象<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">f</code>，但是生成的对象实例是<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">obj</code>，有没有办法将这两个对象统一呢？</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">一个办法就是将<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">obj</code>换成<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">F.prototype</code>。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">function* F() {
  this.a = 1;
  yield this.b = 2;
  yield this.c = 3;
}
var f = F.call(F.prototype);

f.next();  // Object {value: 2, done: false}
f.next();  // Object {value: 3, done: false}
f.next();  // Object {value: undefined, done: true}

f.a // 1
f.b // 2
f.c // 3
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">再将<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">F</code>改成构造函数，就可以对它执行<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">new</code>命令了。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">function* gen() {
  this.a = 1;
  yield this.b = 2;
  yield this.c = 3;
}

function F() {
  return gen.call(gen.prototype);
}

var f = new F();

f.next();  // Object {value: 2, done: false}
f.next();  // Object {value: 3, done: false}
f.next();  // Object {value: undefined, done: true}

f.a // 1
f.b // 2
f.c // 3
</code></pre><h2 id="-" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 24px 0px 16px; padding: 0px 0px 0.3em; top: -900em; left: -900em; box-sizing: border-box; border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(238, 238, 238); line-height: 1.25; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">含义</h2><h3 id="generator-" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 24px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; font-size: 1.25em; box-sizing: border-box; line-height: 1.25; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">Generator与状态机</h3><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">Generator是实现状态机的最佳结构。比如，下面的clock函数就是一个状态机。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">var ticking = true;
var clock = function() {
  if (ticking)
    console.log('Tick!');
  else
    console.log('Tock!');
  ticking = !ticking;
}
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码的clock函数一共有两种状态（Tick和Tock），每运行一次，就改变一次状态。这个函数如果用Generator实现，就是下面这样。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">var clock = function*() {
  while (true) {
    console.log('Tick!');
    yield;
    console.log('Tock!');
    yield;
  }
};
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面的Generator实现与ES5实现对比，可以看到少了用来保存状态的外部变量<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">ticking</code>，这样就更简洁，更安全（状态不会被非法篡改）、更符合函数式编程的思想，在写法上也更优雅。Generator之所以可以不用外部变量保存状态，是因为它本身就包含了一个状态信息，即目前是否处于暂停态。</p><h3 id="generator-" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 24px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; font-size: 1.25em; box-sizing: border-box; line-height: 1.25; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">Generator与协程</h3><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">协程（coroutine）是一种程序运行的方式，可以理解成“协作的线程”或“协作的函数”。协程既可以用单线程实现，也可以用多线程实现。前者是一种特殊的子例程，后者是一种特殊的线程。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;"><span style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; font-weight: 600; box-sizing: border-box;">（1）协程与子例程的差异</span></p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">传统的“子例程”（subroutine）采用堆栈式“后进先出”的执行方式，只有当调用的子函数完全执行完毕，才会结束执行父函数。协程与其不同，多个线程（单线程情况下，即多个函数）可以并行执行，但是只有一个线程（或函数）处于正在运行的状态，其他线程（或函数）都处于暂停态（suspended），线程（或函数）之间可以交换执行权。也就是说，一个线程（或函数）执行到一半，可以暂停执行，将执行权交给另一个线程（或函数），等到稍后收回执行权的时候，再恢复执行。这种可以并行执行、交换执行权的线程（或函数），就称为协程。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">从实现上看，在内存中，子例程只使用一个栈（stack），而协程是同时存在多个栈，但只有一个栈是在运行状态，也就是说，协程是以多占用内存为代价，实现多任务的并行。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;"><span style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; font-weight: 600; box-sizing: border-box;">（2）协程与普通线程的差异</span></p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">不难看出，协程适合用于多任务运行的环境。在这个意义上，它与普通的线程很相似，都有自己的执行上下文、可以分享全局变量。它们的不同之处在于，同一时间可以有多个线程处于运行状态，但是运行的协程只能有一个，其他协程都处于暂停状态。此外，普通的线程是抢先式的，到底哪个线程优先得到资源，必须由运行环境决定，但是协程是合作式的，执行权由协程自己分配。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">由于ECMAScript是单线程语言，只能保持一个调用栈。引入协程以后，每个任务可以保持自己的调用栈。这样做的最大好处，就是抛出错误的时候，可以找到原始的调用栈。不至于像异步操作的回调函数那样，一旦出错，原始的调用栈早就结束。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">Generator函数是ECMAScript 6对协程的实现，但属于不完全实现。Generator函数被称为“半协程”（semi-coroutine），意思是只有Generator函数的调用者，才能将程序的执行权还给Generator函数。如果是完全执行的协程，任何函数都可以让暂停的协程继续执行。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">如果将Generator函数当作协程，完全可以将多个需要互相协作的任务写成Generator函数，它们之间使用yield语句交换控制权。</p><h2 id="-" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 24px 0px 16px; padding: 0px 0px 0.3em; top: -900em; left: -900em; box-sizing: border-box; border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(238, 238, 238); line-height: 1.25; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">应用</h2><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">Generator可以暂停函数执行，返回任意表达式的值。这种特点使得Generator有多种应用场景。</p><h3 id="-1-" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 24px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; font-size: 1.25em; box-sizing: border-box; line-height: 1.25; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">（1）异步操作的同步化表达</h3><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">Generator函数的暂停执行的效果，意味着可以把异步操作写在yield语句里面，等到调用next方法时再往后执行。这实际上等同于不需要写回调函数了，因为异步操作的后续操作可以放在yield语句下面，反正要等到调用next方法时再执行。所以，Generator函数的一个重要实际意义就是用来处理异步操作，改写回调函数。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">function* loadUI() {
  showLoadingScreen();
  yield loadUIDataAsynchronously();
  hideLoadingScreen();
}
var loader = loadUI();
// 加载UI
loader.next()

// 卸载UI
loader.next()
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码表示，第一次调用loadUI函数时，该函数不会执行，仅返回一个遍历器。下一次对该遍历器调用next方法，则会显示Loading界面，并且异步加载数据。等到数据加载完成，再一次使用next方法，则会隐藏Loading界面。可以看到，这种写法的好处是所有Loading界面的逻辑，都被封装在一个函数，按部就班非常清晰。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">Ajax是典型的异步操作，通过Generator函数部署Ajax操作，可以用同步的方式表达。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">function* main() {
  var result = yield request("http://some.url");
  var resp = JSON.parse(result);
    console.log(resp.value);
}

function request(url) {
  makeAjaxCall(url, function(response){
    it.next(response);
  });
}

var it = main();
it.next();
